
## Working i-Ready haxsss
Developed by EpicMods Team 
https://discord.gg/Cs6nMBtNSS  Join our Discord Server.

**How to use
1: Login to Iready
2: Open a lesson.
3: Execute the following code, either by opening the developer console (F12) or creating a bookmarklet:**
